NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
A. Suresh, was born as a male child to M. Arumugam, on 7th July 1990, residing at No. 4/7c, Kalar Patti, Mutthunaicken
Patti (Via), Semmenkoodal Post, Omalur Taluk, Salem District-636 004, After an Elaborate Sexual Reassignment Surgery she has
been living as a female (Reference Dr. P. PARTHA SARATHY, M.S., M.Oh, (Plastic surgery) Government Mohan Kumaramangalam
Medical College Hospital, Salem-636 001]. The through Clinical Examination under Dr. P. PARTHA SARATHY, M.S., M.Oh
(Plastic Surgery) Government Mohan Kumaramangalam Medical College Hospital, Salem-636 001. Shows that I could be treated
as a female. A. Suresh, shall be known as A. KALAISELVI.

Salem,
17th September 2013.

A. SURESH,
